+/**
+ * Loads all application on start, so each module will be available to
+ * required synchronously
+ */
+require([
+    &quot;underscore&quot;,
+    &quot;backbone&quot;,
+    &quot;form2js&quot;,
+    &quot;js2form&quot;,
+    &quot;spin&quot;,
+    &quot;jqgrid&quot;,
+    &quot;jqueryui&quot;,
+    &quot;xdate&quot;,
+    &quot;moment&quot;,
+    &quot;doTimeout&quot;,
+    &quot;handlebars&quot;,
+    &quot;i18next&quot;,

+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/i18nManager&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/Constants&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/EventManager&quot;,

+
+    // Mock project is run without server. Framework requires cookies to be enabled in order to be able to login.
+    // Default CookieHelper.cookiesEnabled() implementation will always return false as cookies cannot be set from local
+    // file. Hence redefining function to return true
+    require('org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/CookieHelper').cookiesEnabled = function () {
+        return true;
+    };
+
+    // Adding stub user
+    localStorage.add('test', {

+define(&quot;org/forgerock/mock/ui/common/delegates/PolicyDelegate&quot;, [
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/Constants&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/AbstractDelegate&quot;
+], function (constants, AbstractDelegate) {
+    var obj = new AbstractDelegate(&quot;&quot;);
+
+    obj.validateProperty = function (baseEntity, args, callback) {
+        /* 
+         * We are calling the validateObject action here instead of validateProperty
+         * because we need to pass in entire object context in order to support policies
+         * which may depend upon other properties.  From the response, we look to see if the 
+         * particular property we are attempting to validate was included in the list of those
+         * with errors.
+         */
+        obj.serviceCall({
+            url: &quot;/&quot; + baseEntity + &quot;?_action=validateObject&quot;,
+            data: JSON.stringify(args.fullObject),
+            type: &quot;POST&quot;,
+            success: function (data) {
+                var haveWeFailed = false;
+                if (data.failedPolicyRequirements) {
+                    _.each(data.failedPolicyRequirements, function (failedReq) {
+                        if (failedReq.property === args.property) {
+                            haveWeFailed = true;
+                            callback({
+                                &quot;result&quot;: false,
+                                &quot;failedPolicyRequirements&quot;: [failedReq]
+                            });
+                        }
+                    });
+                }
+
+                if (!haveWeFailed) {
+                    callback({ &quot;result&quot;: true });
+                }
+            }
+        });
+    };
+
+    return obj;
+});

+/*global define, $*/
+
+/**
+ * Local storage helper.
+ *
+ * @author Eugenia Sergueeva
+ */
+
+define(&quot;org/forgerock/mock/ui/common/main/LocalStorage&quot;, function () {
+    var mockPrefix = 'forgerock-mock-';
+
+    function isLocalStorageSupported() {
+        return typeof localStorage !== 'undefined';
+    }
+
+    return isLocalStorageSupported() ? {
+        /**
+         * Adds data.
+         *
+         * @param key
+         * @param data
+         * @returns {Object} newly added data
+         */
+        add: function (key, data) {
+            if (!this.get(key)) {
+                console.log('Adding item to localStorage: ' + data);
+                localStorage.setItem(mockPrefix + key, JSON.stringify(data));
+                return data;
+            }
+
+            return null;
+        },
+
+        /**
+         * Patches data.
+         *
+         * @param key
+         * @param data
+         * @returns {Object} patched data
+         */
+        patch: function (key, data) {
+            var item = this.get(key);
+            if (item) {
+                var dataLength = data.length;
+                for (var i = 0; i &lt; dataLength; i++) {
+                    item[data[i].field] = data[i].value;
+                }
+                console.log('Patching item in localStorage under key: ' + key);
+                localStorage.setItem(mockPrefix + key, JSON.stringify(item));
+            }
+            return item;
+        },
+
+        /**
+         * Gets data by key.
+         *
+         * @param key
+         * @returns {Object}
+         */
+        get: function (key) {
+            console.log('Getting from localStorage by key: ' + key);
+            return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(mockPrefix + key));
+        },
+
+        /**
+         * Removes data by key.
+         *
+         * @param key
+         * @returns {boolean} whether data was removed
+         */
+        remove: function (key) {
+            console.log('Removing data from localStorage by key: ' + key);
+            return delete localStorage[mockPrefix + key];
+        }
+    } : {
+        add: function () {
+            console.log('LocalStorage is not supported');
+        },
+
+        patch: function () {
+            console.log('LocalStorage is not supported');
+        },
+
+        get: function () {
+            console.log('LocalStorage is not supported');
+        },
+
+        remove: function () {
+            console.log('LocalStorage is not supported');
+        }
+    };
+});
</ins><span class="cx">\ No newline at end of file

+        baseTemplate: &quot;templates/common/MediumBaseTemplate.html&quot;,
+        delegate: userDelegate,

+            conf.forgottenPasswordUserName = this.$el.find(&quot;input[name=email]&quot;).val();

+                this.lock();
+
+                var data = form2js(this.$el.attr(&quot;id&quot;));
+
+                delete data.terms;
+                delete data.passwordConfirm;
+
+                console.log(&quot;ADDING USER: &quot; + JSON.stringify(data));

+                    _id: data.userName,

+                    roles: ['ui-user']
+                });

+                    eventManager.sendEvent(constants.EVENT_USER_SUCCESSFULLY_REGISTERED, { user: data, selfRegistration: true });
+                }, function () {
+                    eventManager.sendEvent(constants.EVENT_DISPLAY_MESSAGE_REQUEST, &quot;userAlreadyExists&quot;);
+                    self.unlock();
+                });
+            }
+        },
+
+        render: function (args, callback) {
+            conf.setProperty(&quot;gotoURL&quot;, null);
+

+                    if (callback) {
+                        callback();
+                    }
+                }, this));
+            });
+        }

+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/Constants&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/AbstractDelegate&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/Configuration&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/EventManager&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/mock/ui/common/main/LocalStorage&quot;
+], function (constants, AbstractDelegate, configuration, eventManager, localStorage) {
+
+    var obj = new AbstractDelegate(&quot;mock/repo/internal/user&quot;);
+
+    obj.usersCallback = null;
+    obj.users = null;
+    obj.numberOfUsers = 0;
+
+    /**
+     * Starting session. Sending username and password to authenticate and returns user's id.
+     */
+    obj.login = function (uid, password, successCallback, errorCallback, errorsHandlers) {
+        var headers = {};
+        headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_USERNAME] = uid;
+        headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_PASSWORD] = password;
+        headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_NO_SESSION] = false;
+
+        obj.getProfile(successCallback, errorCallback, errorsHandlers, headers);
+
+        delete headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_PASSWORD];
+    };
+
+    obj.getUserById = function (id, component, successCallback, errorCallback, errorsHandlers) {
+        this.serviceCall({
+            url: &quot;/&quot; + id,
+            type: &quot;GET&quot;,
+            success: successCallback,
+            error: errorCallback,
+            errorsHandlers: errorsHandlers});
+    };
+
+    obj.checkCredentials = function (password, successCallback, errorCallback) {
+        // not used
+    };
+
+    /**
+     * Checks if logged in and returns users id
+     */
+    obj.getProfile = function (successCallback, errorCallback, errorsHandlers, headers) {
+        if (headers) {
+            var storedUser = localStorage.get(headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_USERNAME]);
+            if (storedUser &amp;&amp; storedUser.password === headers[constants.HEADER_PARAM_PASSWORD]) {
+                successCallback(storedUser);
+            } else {
+                if (errorCallback) {
+                    errorCallback();
+                }
+            }
+        } else {
+            if (errorCallback) {
+                errorCallback();
+            }
+        }
+    };
+
+    /**
+     * Creates new user.
+     */
+    obj.create = function (id, data, successCallback, errorCallback) {
+        if (localStorage.add(data.userName, data)) {
+            successCallback();
+        } else {
+            errorCallback();
+        }
+        return localStorage.add(data.userName, data);
+    };
+
+    obj.getForUserName = function (uid, successCallback, errorCallback) {
+        // not used
+    };
+
+    obj.getForUserID = function (uid, successCallback, errorCallback) {
+        // not used
+    };
+
+    obj.patchUserDifferences = function (oldUserData, newUserData, successCallback, errorCallback, noChangesCallback, errorsHandlers) {
+        console.info(&quot;updating user&quot;);
+
+        var updatedData = obj.getDifferences(oldUserData, newUserData);
+        if (localStorage.patch(configuration.loggedUser._id, updatedData)) {
+            successCallback(updatedData);
+        }
+    };
+
+    obj.updateUser = function (oldUserData, stub, newUserData, successCallback, errorCallback, noChangesCallback) {
+        obj.patchUserDifferences(oldUserData, newUserData, successCallback, errorCallback, noChangesCallback, {
+            &quot;forbidden&quot;: {
+                status: &quot;403&quot;,
+                event: constants.EVENT_USER_UPDATE_POLICY_FAILURE
+            }
+        });
+    };
+
+    obj.patchSelectedUserAttributes = function (id, rev, patchDefinitionObject, successCallback, errorCallback, noChangesCallback) {
+        console.log('changing password');
+        if (localStorage.patch(id, patchDefinitionObject)) {
+            successCallback();
+        }
+    };
+
+    return obj;
+});

+    };

+                conf.globalData.userComponent = user.component;
+                successCallback(user);
+            },
+            function () {
+                if (errorCallback) {

+                }

+                }
+            }
+        );
+    };
+    return obj;

+ * @author mbilski
+ * @author Eugenia Sergueeva
+ */
+define(&quot;org/forgerock/mock/ui/user/profile/ChangeSecurityDataDialog&quot;, [
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/components/Dialog&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/ValidatorsManager&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/Configuration&quot;,
+    &quot;UserDelegate&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/UIUtils&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/main/EventManager&quot;,
+    &quot;org/forgerock/commons/ui/common/util/Constants&quot;
+], function (Dialog, validatorsManager, conf, userDelegate, uiUtils, eventManager, constants) {
+    var ChangeSecurityDataDialog = Dialog.extend({
+        contentTemplate: &quot;templates/mock/ChangeSecurityDataDialogTemplate.html&quot;,
+
+        events: {
+            &quot;click input[type=submit]&quot;: &quot;formSubmit&quot;,
+            &quot;onValidate&quot;: &quot;onValidate&quot;,
+            &quot;customValidate&quot;: &quot;customValidate&quot;,
+            &quot;click .dialogCloseCross img&quot;: &quot;close&quot;,
+            &quot;click input[name='close']&quot;: &quot;close&quot;,
+            &quot;click .dialogContainer&quot;: &quot;stop&quot;,
+            &quot;check_reauth&quot;: &quot;reauth&quot;
+        },
+        reauth: function (event, propertyName) {
+            // we only need to force re-authentication if the properties needing it are one of the two we are prepared to change
+            if (propertyName === &quot;password&quot;) {
+                if (!conf.hasOwnProperty('passwords')) {
+                    this.reauth_required = true;
+                    eventManager.sendEvent(constants.ROUTE_REQUEST, {routeName: &quot;enterOldPassword&quot;});
+                } else {
+                    this.reauth_required = false;
+                }
+            }
+        },
+
+        formSubmit: function (event) {
+            event.preventDefault();
+
+            var patchDefinitionObject = [], element;
+
+            if (validatorsManager.formValidated(this.$el.find(&quot;#passwordChange&quot;))) {
+                patchDefinitionObject.push({operation: &quot;replace&quot;, field: &quot;password&quot;, value: this.$el.find(&quot;input[name=password]&quot;).val()});
+            }
+
+            userDelegate.patchSelectedUserAttributes(conf.loggedUser._id, conf.loggedUser._rev, patchDefinitionObject, _.bind(function (r) {
+                eventManager.sendEvent(constants.EVENT_DISPLAY_MESSAGE_REQUEST, &quot;securityDataChanged&quot;);
+                delete conf.passwords;
+                this.close();
+
+                userDelegate.getProfile(function (user) {
+                    conf.loggedUser = user;
+                });
+
+            }, this));
+        },
+        customValidate: function () {
+
+            if (validatorsManager.formValidated(this.$el.find(&quot;#passwordChange&quot;))) {
+                this.$el.find(&quot;input[type=submit]&quot;).prop('disabled', false);
+            }
+            else {
+                this.$el.find(&quot;input[type=submit]&quot;).prop('disabled', true);
+            }
+
+        },
+        render: function () {
+            this.actions = [];
+            this.addAction($.t(&quot;common.form.update&quot;), &quot;submit&quot;);
+
+            $(&quot;#dialogs&quot;).hide();
+
+            this.show(_.bind(function () {
+                validatorsManager.bindValidators(this.$el, userDelegate.serviceUrl + &quot;/test&quot;, _.bind(function () {
+                    $(&quot;#dialogs&quot;).show();
+                    if (!this.reauth_required) {
+                        this.reloadData();
+                    }
+                }, this));
+
+            }, this));
+
+            this.$el.find(&quot;input[type=submit]&quot;).prop('disabled', true);
+        },
+
+        reloadData: function () {
+            var user = conf.loggedUser, self = this;
+            this.$el.find(&quot;input[name=_id]&quot;).val(conf.loggedUser._id);
+        }
+    });
+
+    return new ChangeSecurityDataDialog();
+});
</ins><span class="cx">\ No newline at end of file

+            }, this));
